2090void msgpack_rpc_init_function_metadata(Dictionary *metadata)
2091{
2092 msgpack_unpacked unpacked;
2093 msgpack_unpacked_init(&unpacked);
2094 if (msgpack_unpack_next(&unpacked,
2095 (const char *)msgpack_metadata,
2096 sizeof(msgpack_metadata),
2097 NULL((void*)0)) != MSGPACK_UNPACK_SUCCESS) {
2098 abort();
2099 }
2100 Object functions;
2101 msgpack_rpc_to_object(&unpacked.data, &functions);
2102 msgpack_unpacked_destroy(&unpacked);
2103 PUT(*metadata, "functions", functions)(*((((*metadata).size == (*metadata).capacity) ? (((*metadata
).capacity = ((*metadata).capacity ? (*metadata).capacity <<
1 : 8), (*metadata).items = xrealloc((*metadata).items, sizeof
((*metadata).items[0]) * (*metadata).capacity)), 0) : 0), ((*
metadata).items + ((*metadata).size++))) = (((KeyValuePair) {
.key = cstr_to_string("functions"), .value = functions })));
2104}

5123static Map(String, MsgpackRpcRequestHandler)Map_String_MsgpackRpcRequestHandler *methods = NULL((void*)0);

5125void msgpack_rpc_add_method_handler(String method, MsgpackRpcRequestHandler handler)
5126{
5127 map_put(String, MsgpackRpcRequestHandler)map_String_MsgpackRpcRequestHandler_put(methods, method, handler);
5128}

5293
5294MsgpackRpcRequestHandler msgpack_rpc_get_handler_for(const char *name,
5295 size_t name_len)
5296{
5297 String m = {
5298 .data=(char *)name,
5299 .size=MIN(name_len, 24)((name_len) < (24) ? (name_len) : (24))
5300 };
5301 MsgpackRpcRequestHandler rv =
5302 map_get(String, MsgpackRpcRequestHandler)map_String_MsgpackRpcRequestHandler_get(methods, m);
5303
5304 if (!rv.fn) {
5305 rv.fn = msgpack_rpc_handle_missing_method;
5306 }
5307
5308 return rv;
5309}
